name:T‚Äçh‚Äço‚Äçm‚Äça‚ÄçZ‚Äç ‚ÄçC‚Äçh‚Äçe‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçg
info:Superior Twin Beds Room
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:3.5
posted:Posted December 6, 2023
msg:The overall experience starting from the shuttle service all the way to the reception and room service were great. This is my second time staying in this hotel. But nothing had change over the year. You can tell that the room was old and definitely will do a lot better with some upgrades. The hair dryer was old and not serving its purpose. The rain shower head was spoiled and you cannot imagine why would you have the alternate shower head pointing directly towards the shower glass door. Water leaking through the glass door causing the entire toilet floor wet. The TV needed to be upgraded too. One good thing to mention, despite the flooring being carpeted, it did not smell bad at all like some other hotels would along the corridor or our room. 

Location wise, think it is great for those who intend to stay in the hotel just to relax and use its facility like the swimming pool and spa just for a night to transit as it is within wall distance to T1 and just a 5 min shuttle ride to T2. Shuttle service is every 30min. But if you do intend to head to city area, then you will have to take a taxi ride of about 40-50min to town which cost us about 90rmb. 

Kudos to the concierge team, the receptionists and the housekeeping team. They were all polite and very keen to help.  

Overall, we did had a great time at the hotel.

posted:Posted May 23, 2023
msg:Pros: The location is a walking distance from the airport Terminal 1 (South Airport).   It provides a free shuttle every 30 minutes to Terminal 2 (North Airport).
          You can take Line 3 Metro (subway), and walk two floors up and walk out to the hotel in about 4-7 minutes.   The breakfast selection is better than Sheraton in Tianhe, Guangzhou.
Cons: As far as the room, I felt like staying at a 3-star+ hotel.   Usually, in a 5-star hotel, they provide shower caps, combs, sewing kits, and toothbrushes.  Here, they handed two toothbrushes at the front desk.  That's all.  I gave 3+ (plus) because it provides the bathrobes and slippers.  The shower door does not close.  Therefore, a lot of water leaks outside the shower.   The safe deposit box's lock does not work.

name:N‚Äç@‚Äç@‚Äç@
info:Superior King Size Bed Room
info:Stayed in August 2022
info:Solo travelers
info:11 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted August 5, 2022
msg:Reception staff (day and night) were welcoming upon arrival and  quick to resolve disturbance caused by other guests at night respectively. Aside from this positive,  given the cost and international brand, the stay was disappointing. While the room was well supplied with usual amenities, it was very small for one person - a couple would arguably be uncomfortable - and the bathroom was ridiculously tiny. Restaurant (U8) staff were polite, helpful, and attentive;,however, the evening buffet (RMB 198) was poor on variety and quality for the price. It was surprising that while the location of the hotel is stated as being within walking distance to the airport, this is somewhat deceiving as guests cannot access the terminals directly because the hotel is actually located outside - specifically between the two terminals, which means a shuttle bus must be taken to reach your terminal. It should be mentioned that again, the staff responsible for the shuttle bus service were excellent. All in all, this is a hotel that is supported by wonderful staff - nevertheless, it is one that I could not recommend because higher quality for the price  is expected from a recognised world class brand.

Name: Pullman Guangzhou Baiyun Airport
Pullman Guangzhou Baiyun Airport Hotel
Location: North of the terminal building of Guangzhou Baiyun International Airport, next to the Airport South Station of Metro Line 3.
Features along the hotel: It is so close to the airport, you can walk to the terminal building. The hotel is connected to Gate 12 of Terminal 1, and provides a shuttle bus to Terminal 2.
